</tr>
<tr>

Yes. It should mainly be talking about this company… wait, because it sounds a bit loud, can you say it again?</td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 有。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Yes.</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 會，我會。而且其實它雖然告訴我這些資訊是有用的，但是它這些東西，因為我看不見它的數據，所以我覺得這是有點類似主觀的想法嗎？這樣子。例如說，他直接跟我說喔這是低 (註: TXT 誤聽為 d)、這是高、這是中，然後有待改善、哪裡不好什麼之類的，但他沒有給我看到那個數據。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Yes, I would. And actually, although the information it tells me is useful, but these things, because I can’t see its data, so I feel it’s a bit like a subjective thought? Like that. For example, it directly tells me oh this is low (Note: TXT misheard as d), this is high, this is medium, then needs improvement, where it’s not good, things like that, but it didn’t show me the data.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 好。那妳有什麼問題想問它嗎？也可以自己打字，還是可以按按鈕都可以。問它什麼都可以問。妳要去上面…上面。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Okay. Do you have any questions you want to ask it? You can also type yourself, or you can press the buttons. You can ask it anything. You need to go up… up.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 妳剛剛問什麼？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> What did you just ask?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 我剛剛問它「我怎麼可以更環保？」</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> I just asked it, “How can I be more environmentally friendly?”</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 那這個內容裡面有什麼妳之前 (註: TXT 用 最近) 不知道的嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Is there anything in this content that you didn’t know before (Note: TXT used “recently”)?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 我之前 (註: TXT 用 最近) 不知道…「考慮購買就」…沒有，其實這些東西我都知道。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Before (Note: TXT used “recently”) I didn’t know… “Consider buying then”… No, actually, I know all these things.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> OK。那妳可以介紹一下它跟妳說什麼嗎？好。妳自己覺得重點在哪裡？妳覺得哪裡重要？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> OK. Can you explain what it told you? Okay. What do you think the main point is? Where do you think is important?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 呃，我覺得重要的有那個吧，「減少購物頻率」，還有「修理而非丟棄」，還有「支持本地產品」，這三個。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Uh, I think the important ones are that, “Reduce shopping frequency,” also “Repair instead of discarding,” and “Support local products,” these three.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 好的。那妳有其他的問題想問嗎？嗯，也可以再次打字 (註: TXT 誤聽為 答次) 問。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Okay. Do you have other questions you want to ask? Hmm, you can also type (Note: TXT misheard as “answer times”) again to ask.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 這個妳問什麼？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> What did you ask about this?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 「欸，我買的產品裡有沒有對我身體有害的化學物質？」</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> “Hey, are there any chemical substances harmful to my body in the products I buy?”</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 喔，然後它跟我說可以告訴它具體的產品或品牌，所以我（下次）是要打字嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Oh, then it told me I can tell it the specific product or brand, so do I need to type (next time)?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 對。好。（看到 interviewee 在打字）妳要寫什麼？ 沒關係。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Yes. Okay. (Sees interviewee typing) What are you writing? It’s okay.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 那如果不需要打字，可以跟它用聲音對話比較好嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> So if typing isn’t needed, would it be better to have a voice conversation with it?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 可以用聲音？好…我覺得目前沒有這個設定。 … 會比較方便一點。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Use voice? Okay… I think currently there isn’t this setting. … It would be a bit more convenient.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 好。妳也可以用英文跟它講喔。好，如果比較方便。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Okay. You can also speak to it in English. Okay, if it’s more convenient.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> （嘗試打英文）好像不太好…喔。嗯…（Me: 妳在找什麼？）我在找那個…那個品牌的英文是什麼…沒關係，那我換一個好了。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> (Tries typing in English) Seems not quite right… Oh. Hmm… (Me: What are you looking for?) I’m looking for the… the English name of that brand… Never mind, I’ll switch to another one.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 那這個（回答）的裡面有什麼妳不知道的嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Is there anything in this (answer) that you didn’t know?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 像其實我不知道口紅裡面會有鉛，然後我也沒有知道鄰苯二甲酸酯這種比較學名一點的化學物質。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Like, actually I didn’t know there could be lead in lipstick, and I also didn’t know about phthalates, this kind of more scientific chemical substance.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 好。那妳剛剛提到這個，妳有什麼感覺嗎？會影響妳的想法還是什麼？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Okay. You mentioned this just now, do you have any feelings about it? Does it influence your thoughts or anything?</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Hmm, I’ll realize maybe I shouldn’t wear makeup so often. Yes.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> 好的。OK。那妳可以幫我回那個Momo那邊。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Okay. OK. Can you help me go back to the Momo page?</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Uh, at the very (Note: TXT misheard as “table”) top, there’s a code, the green one, can you say it out loud for me?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 這個代碼是17LSR。(註: Participant read E7L)</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> This code is 17LSR. (Note: Participant read E7L)</td>

</tr>

</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> (Writing code) 這樣就可以了。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> (Writing code) This should be fine.</td>

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 因為這樣我就可以知道我要怎麼用它。然後因為它也是要插電的，這樣它有寫出來我就會比較知道說要怎麼使用才會比較安全。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Because this way I can know how to use it. And because it also needs to be plugged in, having it written out like this makes me understand better how to use it more safely.</td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Me:</strong> Okay. This one, just typed… is there anything important in the content it gave you?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 我看一下喔。就是他會，他因為他這裡的那個，他這裡舉例的就跟…就會牌子就會比較大，然後我就可以看說這三個，這三個關於環保的，關於環保或是人權管理的部分做了什麼事情。然後這些品牌會比較像是，一般人會參考的。因為剛剛那些就是說碳排放量很低的，可能平常我們要買的時候我們不會想到，但是我們想到這些，然後我們可以之間 (註: 應為 直接) 比較的話其實還不錯。而且他最後也會幫我們統整說誰跟誰在評分上面比較好，然後就是會變成更好的選擇。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Let me see. It will, because here, the examples it gives are like… the brands will be bigger, and then I can see these three, what these three have done regarding environmental protection, or human rights management. And these brands are more like what ordinary people would refer to. Because those ones just now that said low carbon emissions, maybe we wouldn’t think of them when we usually buy, but we think of these, and if we can compare between (Note: “between” likely misspoken, meant “directly”) them, it’s actually quite good. </tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 就是檢查一個產品的可課 (註: 應為 可持續性)…就是不管是買自己買東西或是買家用品，就是一個東西，可持續性。就是，我覺得就是之前會有人說你的消費決定你的生活，就是你要像是比如說像我可能不喜歡就是之前會有一些那種剝削的，使用剝削的棉花的品牌，我可能就不會消費。就是我覺得說聯合抵制或是什麼，這件事情是對公司會有壓力的。那假設我在環保這部分上，然後大家也許注意到這件事情去相對的比較少買，對品牌，對品牌也是硬傷 (註: 應為 影響)。然後品牌就會想，就是知道這件事情，然後來改善這個狀況。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Just checking a product’s class class (Note: Should be “sustainability”)… It’s like whether buying things for myself or buying household goods, just one thing, sustainability. It’s like, I feel like someone said before, “Your consumption determines your world.” It’s like you need to, for example, like maybe I don’t like brands that previously used exploitative, exploited cotton, I might not consume them. It’s just, I feel that boycotting together or something, this matter puts pressure on the company. So suppose in the environmental aspect, and maybe everyone notices this matter and relatively buys less, for the brand, for the brand it’s also a hard injury (Note: Should be “impact”). <td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> This one?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 不是。嗯…你「想看看」嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> No. Um… “Want to take a look”?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 這個啥？但是我看到這種，我就不會選擇這個產品。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> What’s this? But when I see this kind of thing, I won’t choose this product.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 好的。OK。那你幫我看那個最上面的，就是那個投資的部分？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Okay. OK. Can you help me look at the very top one, the investment section?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 投資？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Investment?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 對。那你之前有投資過嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Yes. Have you invested before?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 哦，我之前有看過，但是他現在 AI 幫我列出來的這兩個我不知道。嗯。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Oh, I’ve seen it before, but these two that the AI listed for me now, I don’t know them. Um.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 陳醫師？覺得這是什麼？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Dr. Chen? [Addressing someone else?] What do you think this is?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 他寫代號，應該是就是這間公司的代號，然後底下應該就是他列出來的股票的圖表。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> It writes code, it should be the code for this company, and below should be the stock charts it listed.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 嗯。那你看到這個想要買這個股票嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Um. Seeing this, do you feel like buying this stock?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 我想一下…我看一下…(Looks at chart)…我可能不會買，因為它的波動有點太大了。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Let me think… let me see… (Looks at chart)… I probably wouldn’t buy, because its volatility is a bit too high.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 瞭。好。OK。那你可以幫我 screenshot 這些部分嗎？你覺得重要的部分。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Understood. Okay. OK. Can you help me screenshot these parts? The parts you think are important.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 嗯。(Takes screenshot) 這個產品要…要入鏡嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Um. (Takes screenshot) Does the product need to… be in the shot?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 還是…對對，就是全部你覺得重要的。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Or… yes yes, just everything you think is important.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 可以直接選這裡？咦，但是我可能要先保存它一下，讓它消失。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Can I select directly here? Eh, but I might need to save it first, let it disappear.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> (Takes another screenshot) 還有…嗯…</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> (Takes another screenshot) Also… um…</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 剛剛那個另外一個產品也可以喔。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> The other product from just now is also okay.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 好。嗯。(Takes screenshot) 這個…這邊加一張。好了。然後拍到的產品…這一個。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Okay. Um. (Takes screenshot) This one… add one here. Done. Then the product photographed… this one.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 那為什麼你選這些部分？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Why did you choose these parts?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 嗯…欸？為什麼選這兩個產品嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Um… eh? Why choose these two products?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 不是，就是你剛剛那個 screenshot，為什麼 screenshot 這個部分？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> No, just the screenshot you took, why screenshot this part?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 呃…因為它有列出就是…就是重點，嗯，然後讓我在選擇可以依據它顯示的東西做一下判斷。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Uh… because it listed… just… the key points, um, and then it lets me make a judgment based on the things it displays when choosing.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 好。那最後面的部分，你可以幫我回那個第一個？然後最下面有兩個按鈕，你想要按一個嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Okay. Then the last part, can you help me go back to the first one? Then at the very bottom, there are two buttons, do you want to press one?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 尋找替代上面？查看…嗯…這個。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Find alternatives above? View… um… this one.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 好好。為什麼按這個呢？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Okay okay. Why press this one?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 因為它好像說這是…他還有其他推薦的品牌？所以我選擇了…嗯，這個。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Because it seems to say this is… it has other recommended brands? So I chose… um, this one.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 那他剛剛跟你說什麼？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> What did it tell you just now?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 嗯…他這邊點開來說我們的…哦，它的替代品牌的比較。他有列出來除了我選的富麗森以外，他還有列其他…一二三…其他三種的品牌。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Um… here it opens up saying our… oh, a comparison of its alternative brands. It listed besides the Fujimori I chose, it also listed others… one two three… three other kinds of brands.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 那這些你有聽說過嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Have you heard of these?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 有。飛利浦我有聽過，但印象好像也有，但是這個…不是。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Yes. Philips I’ve heard of, but Impression also seems familiar, but this one… no.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 那你覺得這些品牌怎麼樣？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> What do you think of these brands?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 嗯…這個品牌，我記得飛利浦的品牌我記得還不錯，但是它好像用在其他電器商品。對。然後印象…我忘記是哪一個商品。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Um… this brand, I remember the Philips brand, I remember it’s quite good, but it seems to be used in other electrical appliances. Yes. Then Impression… I forget which product it was.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> 嗯。好。嗯，OK。那你還有什麼問題你想要問 AI 嗎？</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewer:</strong> Um. Okay. Um, OK. Do you have any other questions you want to ask the AI?</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> 目前沒有。</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Interviewee:</strong> Not at the moment.</td>
</tr>
<tr>

## Appendix 2: College Students’ Prototype Self-Testing Survey Data

Due to the large amount data captured by the survey (over 100 people
self-tested the Green Filter app and 32 people filled out the survey
after in-person testing was completed), I’ve chosen to exclude it from
the PDF version of my thesis. The data is available upon request - and
has also been published on Hugging Face as a public dataset here:
https://huggingface.co/datasets/krishaamer/taiwanese-college-students

## Appendix 3: Expert Interviews’ Transcripts

Due to the already too long thesis, I’ve excluded the raw interview
transcripts. The data is available upon request.

## Appendix 4: College Students’ Survey Data

Due to the large amounts of data captured by the initial survey (over
1600 people started the survey, after filtering, leading to over 800
Gen-Z current college students finished it fully), I’ve chosen to
exclude it from the PDF version of my thesis. The data is available upon
request - and has also been published on Hugging Face as a public
dataset here:
https://huggingface.co/datasets/krishaamer/taiwanese-college-students

the software that this research project made use of.

## Appendix 6: Further Reading

Some recommended books on the topics covered in this thesis include, but
are not limited to:

-   R. Buckminster Fuller “Operating Manual for Spaceship Earth”
-   Victor Papanek “Design for the Real World”
-   Jonathan Chapman “Emotionally Durable Design”
-   Carlo Vezzoli “Product-Service System Design for Sustainability”
-   Ezio Manzini “Design, When Everybody Designs”.
